trending bestselling mug** to Printify via API.  \nHere’s the best strategy:\n\n---\n\n### **📌 Step 1: Select a Bestseller Mug Blueprint**\nBased on **Printify's bestsellers**, the **Ceramic Mug (11oz, 15oz)** is a **top-trending product**.  \n\n| 🆔 **Blueprint ID** | **Title**                      | **Category** | **Brand**   |\n| ------------------ | ------------------------------ | ------------ | ----------- |\n| **5**              | Ceramic Mug (11oz, 15oz)       | Drinkware    | Generic     |\n| **22**             | Accent Coffee Mug (11oz, 15oz) | Drinkware    | Generic     |\n| **30**             | Insulated Travel Mug (40oz)    | Drinkware    | Polar Camel |\n\n✅ **Suggested Choice:** **Ceramic Mug (11oz, 15oz) (Blueprint ID: `5`)**  \n- **Reason:** Low cost, high profit, and viral potential on TikTok.  \n\n---\n\n### **📌 Step 2: Prepare Your Data (CSV Format for Bulk Upload)**  \n#### **CSV Example (`printify_mugs.csv`)**:\n```\nTitle,Description,Tags,Price (USD),Image URL,Blueprint ID,Variant ID\n\"Trending Coffee Mug\",\"Best-selling mug with a viral design.\",\"mug, coffee, funny, trending\",12.99,\"https://yourdesignlink.com/design.png\",5,101\n```\n- `Blueprint ID = 5` (Ceramic Mug)\n- `Variant ID = 101` (White Mug)\n\n---\n\n### **📌 Step 3: Bulk Upload Using Printify API**\nThis script will:\n✅ **Load your API Key & Shop IDs**  \n✅ **Upload mugs from a CSV file**  \n✅ **Push the product live on Printify**  \n\n---\n\n### **📜 Python Script for Bulk Upload**\n```python\nimport os\nimport json\nimport requests\nimport csv\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\n\n# Load .env variables\nload_dotenv(dotenv_path=os.path.expanduser(\"~/.env\"))\n\n# Retrieve API Key & Shop Data\nAPI_TOKEN = os.getenv(\"PRINTIFY_API_KEY\")\nSHOP_DATA_RAW = os.getenv(\"PRINTIFY_SHOPS\")\n\n# Ensure environment variable is loaded\nif SHOP_DATA_RAW is None:\n    print(\"❌ ERROR: PRINTIFY_SHOPS not found in environment!\")\n    exit(1)\n\n# Convert JSON string to a dictionary\nSHOP_DATA = json.loads(SHOP_DATA_RAW)\n\n# Choose the TikTok Shop ID\nTIKTOK_SHOP_ID = None\nfor shop_id, name in SHOP_DATA.items():\n    if \"TikTok\" in name:\n        TIKTOK_SHOP_ID = shop_id\n        break\n\nif not TIKTOK_SHOP_ID:\n    print(\"❌ ERROR: No TikTok shop found in your shops list!\")\n    exit(1)\n\n# API URLs\nBASE_URL = f\"https://api.printify.com/v1/shops/{TIKTOK_SHOP_ID}/products.json\"\nHEADERS = {\n    \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {API_TOKEN}\",\n    \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n}\n\ndef upload_mugs_from_csv(csv_file):\n    \"\"\"Uploads mug products from a CSV file to Printify.\"\"\"\n    with open(csv_file, newline='', encoding='utf-8') as file:\n        reader = csv.DictReader(file)\n        for row in reader:\n            product_data = {\n                \"title\": row[\"Title\"],\n                \"description\": row[\"Description\"],\n                \"tags\": row[\"Tags\"].split(\", \"),\n                \"blueprint_id\": int(row[\"Blueprint ID\"]),\n                \"variants\": [\n                    {\n                        \"id\": int(row[\"Variant ID\"]),\n                        \"price\": float(row[\"Price (USD)\"]),\n                        \"is_enabled\": True\n                    }\n                ],\n                \"print_areas\": [\n                    {\n                        \"variant_ids\": [int(row[\"Variant ID\"])],\n                        \"placeholders\": [\n                            {\n                                \"position\": \"front\",\n                                \"images\": [\n                                    {\n                                        \"url\": row[\"Image URL\"],\n                                        \"x\": 0.5,\n                                        \"y\": 0.5,\n                                        \"scale\": 1.0,\n                                        \"angle\": 0\n                                    }\n                                ]\n                            }\n                        ]\n                    }\n                ]\n            }\n\n            response = requests.post(BASE_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=product_data)\n\n            if response.status_code == 201:\n                print(f\"✅ Successfully uploaded: {row['Title']}\")\n            else:\n                print(f\"❌ Failed to upload {row['Title']}: {response.text}\")\n\n# 🚀 Run the bulk upload\nupload_mugs_from_csv(\"printify_mugs.csv\")\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🚀 How to Run the Script**\n1. **Ensure your `.env` file contains:**\n   ```ini\n   PRINTIFY_API_KEY=\"your_printify_api_key\"\n   PRINTIFY_SHOPS='{\"6511744\": \"Etsy\", \"19528660\": \"TikTok\"}'\n   ```\n2. **Create `printify_mugs.csv`** with your product data.\n3. **Run the script:**\n   ```bash\n   python upload_printify_mugs.py\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### **🔍 Expected Output**\n```\n✅ Successfully uploaded: Trending Coffee Mug\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🎯 Why This Works**\n✅ **Uses CSV for bulk product upload**  \n✅ **Targets TikTok Shop only**  \n✅ **Ensures correct Blueprint & Variant IDs**  \n\n🔥 **Now you can scale your Printify mug uploads with automation!** 🚀 Let me know if you need modifications!\n\nTo retrieve the list of available blueprints from Printify, you can use the following Python script. This script sends a GET request to the Printify API's blueprints endpoint and outputs the blueprint IDs along with their titles:\n\n```python\nimport requests\nimport os\n\n# Load your Printify API token from environment variables\nAPI_TOKEN = os.getenv(\"PRINTIFY_API_KEY\")\n\n# Define the endpoint URL\nurl = \"https://api.printify.com/v1/catalog/blueprints.json\"\n\n# Set up the headers with authorization\nheaders = {\n    \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {API_TOKEN}\"\n}\n\n# Send the GET request to the blueprints endpoint\nresponse = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\n\n# Check if the request was successful\nif response.status_code == 200:\n    blueprints = response.json()\n    for blueprint in blueprints:\n        print(f\"Blueprint ID: {blueprint['id']} - Title: {blueprint['title']}\")\nelse:\n    print(f\"Failed to retrieve blueprints. Status code: {response.status_code}\")\n```\n\nEnsure that your `PRINTIFY_API_KEY` is correctly set in your environment variables before running this script. This script will print out each blueprint's ID and title, allowing you to identify the products available for creation through the Printify API. \n\n### **🚀 Fetch Printify Blueprints & Output to CSV**  \n\nThis script will:  \n✅ **Use your API token** to fetch all **Printify blueprints**  \n✅ **Extract relevant details** (ID, title, description, price, variants)  \n✅ **Save everything into a CSV file**  \n\n---\n\n### **📜 Python Script to Fetch & Save Blueprints**\n```python\nimport os\nimport csv\nimport requests\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\n\n# Load .env variables\nload_dotenv(dotenv_path=os.path.expanduser(\"~/.env\"))\n\n# Retrieve API Key\nAPI_TOKEN = os.getenv(\"PRINTIFY_API_KEY\")\n\n# API URL\nBLUEPRINTS_URL = \"https://api.printify.com/v1/catalog/blueprints.json\"\n\n# Headers\nHEADERS = {\n    \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {API_TOKEN}\",\n    \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n}\n\ndef fetch_blueprints():\n    \"\"\"Fetch all Printify blueprints from API\"\"\"\n    response = requests.get(BLUEPRINTS_URL, headers=HEADERS)\n\n    if response.status_code == 200:\n        return response.json()\n    else:\n        print(f\"❌ ERROR: {response.status_code} - {response.text}\")\n        return None\n\ndef save_to_csv(blueprints, filename=\"printify_blueprints.csv\"):\n    \"\"\"Save blueprint data to CSV\"\"\"\n    csv_file_path = os.path.join(\"/mnt/data\", filename)\n    fieldnames = [\"Blueprint ID\", \"Title\", \"Description\", \"Category\", \"Brand\", \"Preview Image\"]\n\n    with open(csv_file_path, mode=\"w\", newline=\"\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as file:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(file, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n\n        for blueprint in blueprints:\n            writer.writerow({\n                \"Blueprint ID\": blueprint[\"id\"],\n                \"Title\": blueprint[\"title\"],\n                \"Description\": blueprint.get(\"description\", \"N/A\"),\n                \"Category\": blueprint.get(\"category\", \"N/A\"),\n                \"Brand\": blueprint.get(\"brand\", \"N/A\"),\n                \"Preview Image\": blueprint.get(\"preview_image\", \"N/A\")\n            })\n\n    print(f\"✅ Blueprints saved to: {csv_file_path}\")\n    return csv_file_path\n\n# 🚀 Run the process\nblueprints = fetch_blueprints()\nif blueprints:\n    csv_path = save_to_csv(blueprints)\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🚀 How to Run the Script**\n1. **Ensure your `.env` file contains your API token**  \n   ```ini\n   PRINTIFY_API_KEY=\"your_printify_api_key\"\n   ```\n2. **Run the script**  \n   ```bash\n   python fetch_printify_blueprints.py\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### **🔍 Expected CSV Output**\n```\nBlueprint You Use for Printify Products?**  \n\nThe **optimal number of mockups** depends on the product type and platform. Here’s a breakdown:\n\n---\n\n### **📜 Recommended Mockups per Product Type**  \n\n| **Product Type**          | **Recommended # of Mockups** | **Why?**                                         |\n| ------------------------- | ---------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------ |\n| **T-Shirts & Hoodies**    | **4-6**                      | Show front, back, lifestyle shots, close-ups     |\n| **Mugs & Drinkware**      | **3-5**                      | Show both sides, top view, lifestyle shots       |\n| **Phone Cases**           | **3-4**                      | Show front, side angles, lifestyle shots         |\n| **Tote Bags**             | **3-5**                      | Show design placement, lifestyle, close-up       |\n| **Stickers**              | **2-4**                      | Show cut-lines, applied mockups, variety pack    |\n| **Canvases & Posters**    | **3-5**                      | Show wall placement, framed/unframed, close-up   |\n| **Pillows & Blankets**    | **4-6**                      | Show flat, folded, on furniture, close-up        |\n| **Candles & Home Decor**  | **3-5**                      | Show label, different angles, lifestyle shots    |\n| **Jewelry & Accessories** | **4-6**                      | Show worn, close-ups, packaging (if available)   |\n| **Pet Products**          | **3-5**                      | Show in use, close-up of design, multiple angles |\n\n---\n\n### **🔥 Best Practices for Mockups**\n✅ **Use Lifestyle Mockups** – People want to see the product in a real-world setting.  \n✅ **Show Different Angles** – Helps customers understand the design placement.  \n✅ **Highlight Close-Up Details** – Showcase print quality and material texture.  \n✅ **Use Consistent Backgrounds** – Keep a professional, cohesive look across listings.  \n✅ **Test Different Mockups for Engagement** – A/B test which images convert best.  \n\n---\n\n### **🎯 How Many Mockups Should You Upload?**\n- **Minimum:** **3-4 mockups per product**\n- **Optimal:** **5-6 mockups for high engagement**\n- **Maximum:** **7+ mockups if the design has variations (colors, angles, etc.)**  \n\n🔥 **Now you know the perfect number of mockups for Printify products!** 🚀 Let me know if you need mockup tools or automation tips!\n\n### **🚀 Refined Printify Bestseller Data for Bulk Upload**  \n\nThis is a **merged like mugs, hoodies, and tote bags **go viral easily**  \n✅ **Trendy aesthetic products** – Vintage **garment-dyed shirts** & **customized pet portraits** appeal to TikTok's user base  \n✅ **Personalized & fast-moving items** – **Stickers, candles, and tote bags** have **high repeat purchase rates**  \n\n🔥 **Now you have a refined CSV ready for your TikTok Printify store!** 🚀 Let me know if you need additional tweaks!\n\n### **Oh, So You Want an AI to Decide What TikTok-Worthy Printify Product Your Random Image Belongs On? Genius.**  \n\nSure! Let’s take your **brilliant** (not at all unnecessary) image analysis script and fuse it with **top-selling Printify products for TikTok**, because clearly, a neural network deciding whether your art belongs on a **trendy hoodie or a scented candle** is what the world was missing.  \n\n---\n\n### **📜 The Ultimate, No-Nonsense Printify Product Matcher**  \n\n```python\nimport cv2\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytesseract\nfrom PIL import Image\nimport os\n\n# Because life is unfair, you need to set this manually for macOS users\npytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = \"/usr/local/bin/tesseract\"  # Adjust if needed\n\n# 🔥 TikTok Printify Bestsellers — aka “What Will Actually Sell”\nPRODUCTS = {\n    \"hoodie\": [\"bold colors\", \"dark tones\", \"statement text\"],\n    \"t-shirt\": [\"minimalist\", \"memes\", \"high contrast\"],\n    \"tote bag\": [\"artistic\", \"neutral tones\", \"simple graphics\"],\n    \"phone case\": [\"vibrant\", \"pop culture\", \"sharp details\"],\n    \"sticker\": [\"high contrast\", \"small details\", \"text-heavy\"],\n    \"candle\": [\"aesthetic\", \"soft colors\", \"cozy themes\"],\n    \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"cozy aesthetics\", \"neutral patterns\"],\n    \"insulated mug\": [\"bold, attention-grabbing\", \"trendy phrases\"],\n    \"kids tee\": [\"fun colors\", \"kid-friendly graphics\", \"cartoon elements\"]\n}\n\ndef get_dominant_color(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts the dominant color from an image, because apparently, that matters now.\"\"\"\n    img = Image.open(image_path).resize((50, 50))  # Resize for \"efficiency\"\n    img_array = np.array(img).reshape(-1, 3)\n    unique, counts = np.unique(img_array, axis=0, return_counts=True)\n    dominant_color = unique[counts.argmax()]  # Because majority rules, right?\n    return tuple(dominant_color)\n\ndef detect_text(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts text from an image, because if there’s no text, is it even worth selling?\"\"\"\n    img = cv2.imread(image_path)\n    gray = cv2.cvtColor(img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2GRAY)\n    text = pytesseract.image_to_string(gray)\n    return text.strip() if text else None\n\ndef match_product(dominant_color, text):\n    \"\"\"Decides which Printify product your masterpiece belongs on. AI is truly wasted on this.\"\"\"\n    r, g, b = dominant_color\n    category = \"unknown\"\n\n    if text:\n        # TikTok loves text-heavy stuff, so stickers and t-shirts are your best bet\n        category = \"sticker\" if len(text) < 50 else \"t-shirt\"\n    \n    elif r > g and r > b:\n        category = \"hoodie\"  # Red tones = \"Buy Me Now\" urgency\n    \n    elif g > r and g > b:\n        category = \"candle\"  # Green = *essential oils & wellness influencers screeching in the distance*\n    \n    elif b > r and b > g:\n        category = \"phone case\"  # Blue = slick, trendy, overpriced\n    \n    elif r > 200 and g > 200 and b > 200:\n        category = \"tote bag\"  # Light tones = aesthetic, reusable, and pretending to be eco-friendly\n    \n    elif r < 50 and g < 50 and b < 50:\n        category = \"plush blanket\"  # Dark = cozy, mysterious, probably Tumblr-core\n    \n    else:\n        category = \"t-shirt\"  # The catch-all because people will wear anything with the right hype.\n\n    return category\n\ndef main(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Runs the full analysis and makes a questionable judgment call.\"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n🔍 **AI is About to Judge Your Image...**\")\n\n    if not os.path.exists(image_path):\n        print(\"❌ Error: Your 'art' was not found. Please try harder.\")\n        return\n\n    dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n    text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n\n    print(f\"🎨 **Dominant Color:** {dominant_color}\")\n    print(f\"🔤 **Text Detected:** {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n\n    best_product = match_product(dominant_color, text_detected)\n    \n    print(f\"\\n✅ **Recommended Printify Product for Maximum TikTok Engagement:** {best_product.upper()}\")\n    print(f\"💡 **Why?** {PRODUCTS.get(best_product, 'Best fit based on color, trend, and the TikTok hype machine.')}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    image_path = input(\"📂 **Drop your image file path here and let AI take control of your Printify destiny:** \").strip()\n    main(image_path)\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🚀 What This Does**\n- **Analyzes your image** (because colors and text somehow determine product success)  \n- **Matches it with Printify’s top TikTok products** (since we all know trends rule everything)  \n- **Gives you a snarky recommendation** so you can **pretend AI is doing all the work**  \n\n🔥 **Now go forth and let AI monetize your creativity.** 🚀 If this flops, blame the algorithm, not me.\n\n### **🚀 Now You Want Choices? Fine. Here’s Your Overly Customizable Printify AI Tool.**  \nYou get **two options** because I guess just picking TikTok or Etsy manually was too hard.  \n\n---\n\n### **📜 New & Improved Printify AI Matcher**\n```python\nimport cv2\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytesseract\nfrom PIL import Image\nimport os\n\n# Because macOS users need extra hand-holding\npytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = \"/usr/local/bin/tesseract\"  # Adjust if needed\n\n# 🔥 TikTok vs Etsy Bestsellers – Because Your Platform Choice Apparently Matters\nPLATFORMS = {\n    \"tiktok\": {\n        \"hoodie\": [\"bold colors\", \"dark tones\", \"statement text\"],\n        \"t-shirt\": [\"minimalist\", \"memes\", \"high contrast\"],\n        \"tote bag\": [\"artistic\", \"neutral tones\", \"simple graphics\"],\n        \"phone case\": [\"vibrant\", \"pop culture\", \"sharp details\"],\n        \"sticker\": [\"high contrast\", \"small details\", \"text-heavy\"],\n        \"candle\": [\"aesthetic\", \"soft colors\", \"cozy themes\"],\n        \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"cozy aesthetics\", \"neutral patterns\"],\n    },\n    \"etsy\": {\n        \"mug\": [\"custom text\", \"personalized gifts\", \"vintage aesthetics\"],\n        \"wedding candle\": [\"engraved\", \"soft colors\", \"sentimental\"],\n        \"necklace\": [\"delicate\", \"custom name\", \"elegant\"],\n        \"cutting board\": [\"engraved wood\", \"kitchen aesthetics\", \"gift-ready\"],\n        \"pet portrait\": [\"watercolor\", \"hand-drawn look\", \"custom pet art\"],\n        \"doormat\": [\"funny text\", \"personalized\", \"home decor\"],\n    }\n}\n\ndef get_dominant_color(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts the dominant color from an image, because that’s a thing now.\"\"\"\n    img = Image.open(image_path).resize((50, 50))  # Because efficiency™\n    img_array = np.array(img).reshape(-1, 3)\n    unique, counts = np.unique(img_array, axis=0, return_counts=True)\n    dominant_color = unique[counts.argmax()]  # Majority rules, deal with it\n    return tuple(dominant_color)\n\ndef detect_text(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts text, because words = $$$.\"\"\"\n    img = cv2.imread(image_path)\n    gray = cv2.cvtColor(img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2GRAY)\n    text = pytesseract.image_to_string(gray)\n    return text.strip() if text else None\n\ndef match_product(platform, dominant_color, text):\n    \"\"\"Decides whether your masterpiece belongs on TikTok or Etsy products.\"\"\"\n    r, g, b = dominant_color\n    category = \"unknown\"\n\n    if platform not in PLATFORMS:\n        print(\"❌ ERROR: Pick a real platform next time.\")\n        return category\n\n    PRODUCTS = PLATFORMS[platform]\n\n    if text:\n        category = \"sticker\" if len(text) < 50 else \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"mug\"\n\n    elif r > g and r > b:\n        category = \"hoodie\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"doormat\"\n\n    elif g > r and g > b:\n        category = \"candle\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"wedding candle\"\n\n    elif b > r and b > g:\n        category = \"phone case\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"necklace\"\n\n    elif r > 200 and g > 200 and b > 200:\n        category = \"tote bag\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"cutting board\"\n\n    else:\n        category = \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"pet portrait\"\n\n    return category\n\ndef process_directory(directory_path, platform):\n    \"\"\"Scans an entire directory because one image at a time is too slow for your Printify empire.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.isdir(directory_path):\n        print(\"❌ Error: Your directory does not exist. Try harder.\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 **Scanning Directory for {platform.upper()} Products:** {directory_path}\")\n\n    image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(directory_path) if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp'))]\n\n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"⚠️ No valid images found. Maybe try adding some?\")\n        return\n\n    for file in image_files:\n        image_path = os.path.join(directory_path, file)\n        print(f\"\\n🔍 **Processing Image:** {file}\")\n\n        dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n        text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n\n        print(f\"🎨 **Dominant Color:** {dominant_color}\")\n        print(f\"🔤 **Text Detected:** {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n\n        best_product = match_product(platform, dominant_color, text_detected)\n        \n        print(f\"\\n✅ **Recommended {platform.capitalize()} Product:** {best_product.upper()}\")\n        print(f\"💡 **Why?** {PLATFORMS[platform].get(best_product, 'Best match based on color, text, and trendiness.')}\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for Etsy or TikTok, then scans a directory.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 **Enter the directory path with your designs:** \").strip()\n    platform = input(\"📱 **Choose your marketplace (etsy/tiktok):** \").strip().lower()\n\n    process_directory(directory_path, platform)\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🚀 What’s New?**\n✅ **Now lets you choose between Etsy & TikTok** (*because personalization is everything*)  \n✅ **Scans an entire directory** (*because batch processing = efficiency*)  \n✅ **Still lets AI judge your art’s worth** (*because humans are obsolete*)  \n\n🔥 **Now go forth and automate your way to Printify domination.** 🚀  \n*(Just don’t blame me when your AI-picked design flops.)*\n\n### **🚀 Now You Want a Fancy Directory Prompt for Etsy vs. TikTok?      \"cutting board\": [\"engraved wood\", \"kitchen aesthetics\", \"gift-ready\"],\n        \"pet portrait\": [\"watercolor\", \"hand-drawn look\", \"custom pet art\"],\n        \"doormat\": Image.open(image_path).resize((50, 50))\n    img_array = np.array(img).reshape(-1, 3)\n    unique, counts = np.unique(img_array, axis=0, return_counts=True)\n    dominant_color = You're embarrassing us.\")\n        return category\n\n    PRODUCTS = PLATFORMS[platform]\n\n    if text:\n        category = \"sticker\" if len(text) < 50 else \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"mug\"\n\n    elif r > g and r > b:\n        category = \"hoodie\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"doormat\"\n\n    elif g > r and g > b:\n        category = \"candle\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"wedding candle\"\n\n    elif b > r and b > g:\n        category = \"phone case\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"necklace\"\n\n    elif r > 200 and g > 200 and b > 200:\n        category = \"tote bag\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"cutting board\"\n\n    else:\n        category = \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"pet portrait\"\n\n    return category\n\ndef process_directory(directory_path, platform):\n    \"\"\"Scans an entire directory because batch processing = profit.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.isdir(directory_path):\n        print(\"❌ ERROR: Your directory is missing. Just like your business plan.\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 **Scanning Directory for {platform.upper()} Products:** {directory_path}\")\n\n    image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(directory_path) if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp'))]\n\n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"⚠️ No valid images found. Maybe add some?\")\n        return\n\n    for file in image_files:\n        image_path = os.path.join(directory_path, file)\n        print(f\"\\n🔍 **Processing Image:** {file}\")\n\n        dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n        text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n\n        print(f\"🎨 **Dominant Color:** {dominant_color}\")\n        print(f\"🔤 **Text Detected:** {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n\n        best_product = match_product(platform, dominant_color, text_detected)\n        \n        print(f\"\\n✅ **Recommended {platform.capitalize()} Product:** {best_product.upper()}\")\n        print(f\"💡 **Why?** {PLATFORMS[platform].get(best_product, 'Best guess based on trends and AI snobbery.')}\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for Etsy or TikTok, then scans a directory.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 **Enter the directory path with your designs:** \").strip()\n    platform = input(\"📱 **Choose your marketplace (etsy/tiktok):** \").strip().lower()\n\n    process_directory(directory_path, platform)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🔥 What’s New?**\n✅ **Prompts you for a directory path** (*because automation is king*)  \n✅ **Forces you to pick Etsy or TikTok** (*so you don’t accidentally try to sell stickers on Etsy like a fool*)  \n✅ **Scans an entire folder** (*because bulk processing is the only way to win*)  \n✅ **Gives AI-powered snark while doing it** (*because why not?*)  \n\n🔥 **Go forth, automate your Printify empire, and let AI tell you what to sell.** 🚀  \n*(If it fails, just say it was an \"A/B test.\")*\n\n### **🚀 Now You Want Auto-Named CSV Exports? Fine.**  \nYou asked for **full automation**, so now this script will:  \n✅ **Analyze an entire directory** (*because manual selection is for peasants*)  \n✅ **Choose between Etsy & TikTok** (*because clearly, you can’t decide yourself*)  \n✅ **Auto-generate a CSV file** with a filename based on your **folder name & date** (*because why do it manually?*)  \n\n---\n\n### **📜 The Ultimate Printify AI Auto-Categorizer & CSV Generator**\n```python\nimport os\nimport csv\nimport cv2\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytesseract\nfrom PIL import Image\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# Because macOS users always have to be different\npytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = \"/usr/local/bin/tesseract\"\n\n# 🔥 Printify Bestsellers - Etsy vs TikTok\nPLATFORMS = {\n    \"tiktok\": {\n        \"hoodie\": [\"bold colors\", \"dark tones\", \"statement text\"],\n        \"t-shirt\": [\"minimalist\", \"memes\", \"high contrast\"],\n        \"tote bag\": [\"artistic\", \"neutral tones\", \"simple graphics\"],\n        \"phone case\": [\"vibrant\", \"pop culture\", \"sharp details\"],\n        \"sticker\": [\"high contrast\", \"small details\", \"text-heavy\"],\n        \"candle\": [\"aesthetic\", \"soft colors\", \"cozy themes\"],\n        \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"cozy aesthetics\", \"neutral patterns\"],\n    },\n    \"etsy\": {\n        \"mug\": [\"custom text\", \"personalized gifts\", \"vintage aesthetics\"],\n        \"wedding candle\": [\"engraved\", \"soft colors\", \"sentimental\"],\n        \"necklace\": [\"delicate\", \"custom name\", \"elegant\"],\n        \"cutting board\": [\"engraved wood\", \"kitchen aesthetics\", \"gift-ready\"],\n        \"pet portrait\": [\"watercolor\", \"hand-drawn look\", \"custom pet art\"],\n        \"doormat\": [\"funny text\", \"personalized\", \"home decor\"],\n    }\n}\n\ndef get_dominant_color(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts the dominant color from an image.\"\"\"\n    img = Image.open(image_path).resize((50, 50))\n    img_array = np.array(img).reshape(-1, 3)\n    unique, counts = np.unique(img_array, axis=0, return_counts=True)\n    return tuple(unique[counts.argmax()])  # Most common color\n\ndef detect_text(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts text from an image using OCR.\"\"\"\n    img = cv2.imread(image_path)\n    gray = cv2.cvtColor(img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2GRAY)\n    text = pytesseract.image_to_string(gray)\n    return text.strip() if text else None\n\ndef match_product(platform, dominant_color, text):\n    \"\"\"Matches the image with a Printify product.\"\"\"\n    r, g, b = dominant_color\n    category = \"unknown\"\n\n    if platform not in PLATFORMS:\n        print(\"❌ ERROR: Invalid platform. Try again.\")\n        return category\n\n    PRODUCTS = PLATFORMS[platform]\n\n    if text:\n        category = \"sticker\" if len(text) < 50 else \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"mug\"\n\n    elif r > g and r > b:\n        category = \"hoodie\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"doormat\"\n\n    elif g > r and g > b:\n        category = \"candle\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"wedding candle\"\n\n    elif b > r and b > g:\n        category = \"phone case\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"necklace\"\n\n    elif r > 200 and g > 200 and b > 200:\n        category = \"tote bag\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"cutting board\"\n\n    else:\n        category = \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"pet portrait\"\n\n    return category\n\ndef process_directory(directory_path, platform):\n    \"\"\"Scans an entire directory and saves results as a CSV.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.isdir(directory_path):\n        print(\"❌ ERROR: Invalid directory. Try again.\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 Scanning Directory for {platform.upper()} Products: {directory_path}\")\n\n    image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(directory_path) if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp'))]\n    \n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"⚠️ No valid images found. Maybe add some?\")\n        return\n\n    # Auto-generate CSV filename\n    folder_name = os.path.basename(os.path.normpath(directory_path))\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d_%H%M\")\n    csv_filename = f\"{folder_name}_{platform}_{timestamp}.csv\"\n    csv_path = os.path.join(directory_path, csv_filename)\n\n    # Prepare CSV file\n    fieldnames = [\"File Name\", \"Dominant Color\", \"Detected Text\", \"Recommended Product\"]\n    with open(csv_path, mode='w', newline='') as csv_file:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n\n        for file in image_files:\n            image_path = os.path.join(directory_path, file)\n            print(f\"\\n🔍 Processing Image: {file}\")\n\n            dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n            text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n            best_product = match_product(platform, dominant_color, text_detected)\n\n            print(f\"🎨 Dominant Color: {dominant_color}\")\n            print(f\"🔤 Text Detected: {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n            print(f\"\\n✅ Recommended {platform.capitalize()} Product: {best_product.upper()}\")\n\n            # Write to CSV\n            writer.writerow({\n                \"File Name\": file,\n                \"Dominant Color\": str(dominant_color),\n                \"Detected Text\": text_detected if text_detected else \"None\",\n                \"Recommended Product\": best_product.upper()\n            })\n\n    print(f\"\\n📜 CSV File Saved: {csv_path}\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for Etsy or TikTok, then scans a directory and saves results.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 Enter the directory path with your designs: \").strip()\n    platform = input(\"📱 Choose your\n\n### **🚀 Now Featuring: Automated Bestseller Matching for Etsy & TikTok!**  \nBecause of course, you need **AI to  \n\n---\n\n### **📜 The Ultimate Etsy & TikTok Bestseller Product Categorizer**\n```python\nimport os\nimport csv\nimport cv2\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytesseract\nfrom PIL import Image\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# Because macOS users need extra setup\npytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = \"/usr/local/bin/tesseract\"\n\n# 🔥 Printify Bestsellers - Etsy vs TikTok (Updated for     \"tote bag\": [\"artistic\", \"neutral tones\", \"simple graphics\"],\n        \"phone case\": [\"vibrant\", \"pop culture\", \"sharp details\"],\n        \"sticker\": [\"high contrast\", \"small details\", \"text-heavy\"],\n        \"candle\": [\"aesthetic\", \"soft colors\", \"cozy themes\"],\n        \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"cozy aesthetics\", \"neutral patterns\"],\n    },\n    \"etsy\": {\n        \"mug\": [\"custom text\", \"personalized gifts\", \"vintage aesthetics\"],\n        \"wedding candle\": [\"engraved\", \"soft colors\", \"sentimental\"],\n        \"necklace\": return_counts=True)\n    return tuple(unique[counts.argmax()])  # Majority rules\n\ndef detect_text(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts text because apparently, custom text = sales.\"\"\"\n    img = dominant_color, text):\n    \"\"\"Matches the image with a Printify product based on current Etsy & TikTok trends.\"\"\"\n    r, g, b = dominant_color\n    category = \"unknown\"\n\n    if platform not in PLATFORMS:\n        print(\"❌ ERROR: Invalid platform. Try again.\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 Scanning Directory for {platform.upper()} Bestsellers: {directory_path}\")\n\n    image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(directory_path) if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp'))]\n\n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"⚠️ No valid images found. Try again.\")\n        return\n\n    # Auto-generate CSV filename\n    folder_name = os.path.basename(os.path.normpath(directory_path))\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d_%H%M\")\n writer.writeheader()\n\n        for file in image_files:\n            image_path = os.path.join(directory_path, file)\n            print(f\"\\n🔍 Processing Image: {file}\")\n\n            dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n            text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n            best_product = match_product(platform, dominant_color, text_detected)\n\n            print(f\"🎨 Dominant Color: {dominant_color}\")\n            print(f\"🔤 Text Detected: {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n            print(f\"\\n✅ Recommended {platform.capitalize()} Bestseller: {best_product.upper()}\")\n\n            # Write to CSV\n            writer.writerow({\n                \"File Name\": file,\n                \"Dominant Color\": str(dominant_color),\n                \"Detected Text\": text_detected if text_detected else \"None\",\n                \"Recommended Product\": best_product.upper()\n            })\n\n    print(f\"\\n📜 CSV File Saved: {csv_path}\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for Etsy or TikTok, scans a directory, and saves results.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 Enter the directory path with your designs: \").strip()\n    platform = input(\"📱 Choose your marketplace (etsy/tiktok): \").strip().lower()\n\n    process_directory(directory_path, platform)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🔥 What’s New?**\n✅ **Updated Etsy bestsellers** (*because apparently, selling mugs and wedding candles is a goldmine*)  \n✅ **Auto-names your CSV** with the **folder name & candles.\", \"Home & Living\", \"Printed Mint\", 6.57, 5.50, \"2 sizes\", \"2 colors\", \"Printed Mint\"],\n    [SF000, \"Unisex Midweight Softstyle Fleece Crewneck Sweatshirt\", \"Midweight fleece sweatshirt, perfect for custom prints.\", \"Apparel\", \"GildanSF000\", 18.94, 13.93, \"7 sizes\", \"16 colors\", 4],\n    [AOP, \"Unisex Cut & Sew Tee (AOP)\", \"Premium cut & sew t-shirt.\", \"Apparel\", \"Generic\", 21.78, 16.02, \"6 sizes\", \"2 colors\", \"MWW On Demand\"],\n    [30, \"Insulated Travel Mug, 40oz\", \"Perfect for keeping drinks warm or cold, with custom designs.\", \"Drinkware\", \"Polar Camel\", 32.81, 24.14, \"1 size\", \"8 colors\", \"Fulfill Engine\"]\n]\n\ndef generate_csv(directory_path):\n    \"\"\"Creates a CSV file for Etsy bestsellers.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.isdir(directory_path):\n        print(\"❌ ERROR: Your directory doesn’t exist. Try again.\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 Generating CSV for Etsy Bestsellers: {directory_path}\")\n\n    # Auto-generate CSV filename\n    folder_name = os.path.basename(os.path.normpath(directory_path))\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d_%H%M\")\n    csv_filename = f\"{folder_name}_etsy_bestsellers_{timestamp}.csv\"\n    csv_path = os.path.join(directory_path, csv_filename)\n\n    # Prepare CSV file\n    fieldnames = [\"Blueprint ID\", \"Title\", \"Description\", \"Category\", \"Brand\", \"Price (USD)\", \"Premium Price (USD)\", \"Sizes\", \"Colors\", \"Providers\"]\n    with open(csv_path, mode='w', newline='') as csv_file:\n        writer = csv.writer(csv_file)\n        writer.writerow(fieldnames)\n        writer.writerows(ETSY_BESTSELLERS)\n\n    print(f\"\\n📜 CSV File Saved: {csv_path}\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for directory and saves the Etsy bestseller list.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 Enter the directory path where you want to save the CSV: \").strip()\n    generate_csv(directory_path)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n---\n\n### **🔥 What’s New?**\n✅ process_directory(directory_path, platform):\n    \"\"\"Scans an entire directory because one image at a time is too slow for your Printify empire.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.isdir(directory_path):\n        print(\"❌ Error: Your directory does not exist. Try harder.\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 **Scanning Directory for {platform.upper()} Products:** {directory_path}\")\n\n    image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(directory_path) if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp'))]\n\n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"⚠️ No valid images found. Maybe try adding some?\")\n        return\n\n    for file in image_files:\n        image_path = os.path.join(directory_path, file)\n        print(f\"\\n🔍 **Processing Image:** {file}\")\n\n        dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n        text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n\n        print(f\"🎨 **Dominant Color:** {dominant_color}\")\n        print(f\"🔤 **Text Detected:** {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n\n        print(f\"\\n✅ **Recommended {platform.capitalize()} Product:** Check Etsy Bestsellers List.\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for Etsy or TikTok, then scans a directory.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 **Enter the directory path with your designs:** \").strip()\n    platform = input(\"📱 **Choose your marketplace (etsy/tiktok):** \").strip().lower()\n\n    process_directory(directory_path, platform)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n✅ Etsy **bestsellers list updated** with **real Printify data**  \n✅ **TikTok & Etsy analysis mode**  \n✅ **Automated product recommendations**\n\nUnfortunately, I cannot process or analyze the images directly due to system restrictions. This version integrates more robust logic for product matching, better error handling, and CSV exporting for analysis.\n\n---\n\n### Full Script: Improved Etsy & TikTok Bestseller Analysis\n\n```python\nimport os\nimport csv\nimport cv2\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytesseract\nfrom PIL import Image\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# Configure Tesseract for macOS (adjust for your system if needed)\npytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = \"/usr/local/bin/tesseract\"\n\n# 🎯 Etsy & TikTok Bestsellers\nPLATFORMS = {\n    \"tiktok\": {\n        \"hoodie\": [\"bold colors\", \"dark tones\", \"statement text\"],\n        \"t-shirt\": [\"minimalist\", \"memes\", \"high contrast\"],\n        \"tote bag\": [\"artistic\", \"neutral tones\", \"simple graphics\"],\n        \"phone case\": [\"vibrant\", \"pop culture\", \"sharp details\"],\n        \"sticker\": [\"high contrast\", \"small details\", \"text-heavy\"],\n        \"candle\": [\"aesthetic\", \"soft colors\", \"cozy themes\"],\n        \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"cozy aesthetics\", \"neutral patterns\"],\n    },\n    \"etsy\": {\n        \"ceramic mug\": [\"custom text\", \"personalized gifts\", \"vintage aesthetics\"],\n        \"cotton tee\": [\"affordable\", \"durable\", \"versatile for daily wear\"],\n        \"crewneck sweatshirt\": [\"classic style\", \"warmth\", \"perfect for custom designs\"],\n        \"jersey tee\": [\"soft material\", \"stylish\", \"great for casual fashion\"],\n        \"garment-dyed t-shirt\": [\"premium look\", \"trendy\", \"youth appeal\"],\n        \"hooded sweatshirt\": [\"cozy\", \"seasonal favorite\", \"customizable\"],\n        \"scented candle\": [\"relaxation\", \"premium home decor\", \"giftable\"],\n        \"tote bag\": [\"eco-friendly\", \"practical\", \"ideal for custom graphics\"],\n        \"matte canvas\": [\"artistic\", \"premium home decor\", \"custom prints\"],\n        \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"comfort\", \"perfect for gifts\"],\n    }\n}\n\n# 📸 Mockup Guide – Recommendations by Product Type\nMOCKUP_GUIDE = {\n    \"hoodie\": [\"front view\", \"back view\", \"close-up\"],\n    \"t-shirt\": [\"front view\", \"back view\", \"lifestyle\"],\n    \"tote bag\": [\"angled view\", \"close-up\"],\n    \"phone case\": [\"front view\", \"side view\"],\n    \"sticker\": [\"sheet view\", \"individual close-up\"],\n    \"candle\": [\"top view\", \"ambient setting\"],\n    \"plush blanket\": [\"folded view\", \"lifestyle\"],\n    \"ceramic mug\": [\"front view\", \"top view\", \"lifestyle\"],\n}\n\ndef get_dominant_color(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts the dominant color from an image.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        img = Image.open(image_path).resize((50, 50))  # Optimize processing\n        img_array = np.array(img).reshape(-1, 3)\n        unique, counts = np.unique(img_array, axis=0, return_counts=True)\n        dominant_color = unique[counts.argmax()]  # Most common color\n        return tuple(dominant_color)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"❌ Error extracting dominant color: {e}\")\n        return None\n\ndef detect_text(image_path):\n    \"\"\"Extracts text from an image using OCR.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        img = cv2.imread(image_path)\n        gray = cv2.cvtColor(img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2GRAY)\n        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(gray)\n        return text.strip() if text else None\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"❌ Error detecting text: {e}\")\n        return None\n\ndef match_product(platform, dominant_color, text):\n    \"\"\"Matches the image to the best product based on the platform.\"\"\"\n    PRODUCTS = PLATFORMS.get(platform, {})\n    r, g, b = dominant_color if dominant_color else (0, 0, 0)\n    category = \"unknown\"\n\n    if text:\n        if platform == \"etsy\" and \"custom\" in text.lower():\n            category = \"ceramic mug\"\n        elif platform == \"tiktok\":\n            category = \"sticker\" if len(text) < 50 else \"t-shirt\"\n\n    elif r > g and r > b:\n        category = \"hoodie\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"garment-dyed t-shirt\"\n    elif g > r and g > b:\n        category = \"candle\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"scented candle\"\n    elif b > r and b > g:\n        category = \"phone case\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"necklace\"\n    elif r > 200 and g > 200 and b > 200:\n        category = \"tote bag\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"cutting board\"\n\n    return category\n\ndef process_directory(directory_path, platform):\n    \"\"\"Processes a directory of images and provides recommendations.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.isdir(directory_path):\n        print(\"❌ Error: Directory not found.\")\n        return\n\n    output_file = f\"product_recommendations_{platform}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.csv\"\n\n    print(f\"\\n📂 **Processing Images in Directory:** {directory_path}\")\n    print(f\"📝 Recommendations will be saved to: {output_file}\")\n\n    image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(directory_path) if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp'))]\n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"⚠️ No valid image files found. Exiting.\")\n        return\n\n    with open(output_file, mode=\"w\", newline=\"\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.writer(csvfile)\n        writer.writerow([\"Image Name\", \"Dominant Color\", \"Detected Text\", \"Recommended Product\", \"Mockup Suggestions\"])\n\n        for file in image_files:\n            image_path = os.path.join(directory_path, file)\n            print(f\"\\n🔍 **Processing Image:** {file}\")\n\n            dominant_color = get_dominant_color(image_path)\n            text_detected = detect_text(image_path)\n            recommended_product = match_product(platform, dominant_color, text_detected)\n            mockups = MOCKUP_GUIDE.get(recommended_product, \"General mockups\")\n\n            print(f\"🎨 Dominant Color: {dominant_color}\")\n            print(f\"🔤 Detected Text: {text_detected if text_detected else 'None'}\")\n            print(f\"✅ Recommended Product: {recommended_product.upper()}\")\n            print(f\"📸 Suggested Mockups: {', '.join(mockups) if mockups else 'N/A'}\")\n\n            writer.writerow([file, dominant_color, text_detected, recommended_product, \", \".join(mockups) if mockups else \"N/A\"])\n\n    print(\"\\n✅ **Processing Complete!** Check the output CSV for details.\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Prompts user for input and processes a directory of images.\"\"\"\n    directory_path = input(\"📂 Enter the directory path with your designs: \").strip()\n    platform = input(\"📱 Choose your marketplace (etsy/tiktok): \").strip().lower()\n\n    if platform not in PLATFORMS:\n        print(\"❌ Invalid platform. Choose 'etsy' or 'tiktok'.\")\n        return\n\n    process_directory(directory_path, platform)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n---\n\n### Key Improvements:\n1. **Error Handling**:\n   - Wrapped critical functions (`get_dominant_color`, `detect_text`) with `try-except` for robustness.\n\n2. **CSV Export**:\n   - Results are saved to a timestamped CSV file for easy analysis.\n\n3. **Mockup Recommendations**:\n   - Provides mockup suggestions based on the recommended product type.\n\n4. **Dynamic Platform Matching**:\n   - Recommendations vary depending on whether the user selects \"Etsy\" or \"TikTok.\"\n\n5. **User-Friendly Output**:\n   - Clearly displays dominant color, detected text, recommended product, and mockup suggestions.\n\n### Example Output in CSV:\n| Image Name    | Dominant Color  | Detected Text      | Recommended Product | Mockup Suggestions              |\n| ------------- | --------------- | ------------------ | ------------------- | ------------------------------- |\n| `design1.png` | (255, 200, 100) | \"Custom Text Here\" | Ceramic Mug         | front view, top view, lifestyle |\n| `design2.jpg` | (120, 80, 220)  | None               | Hoodie              | front view, back view, close-up |\n\nThis version is flexible, scalable, and provides all the key functionalities to streamline your Etsy or TikTok product analysis workflow.\n\nThis is a polished script with robust error handling, efficient batch processing, and logging to CSV. It ensures that images are processed based on user-defined preferences for resizing or upscaling. Here's how it works and what makes it stand out:\n\n---\n\n### Key Features:\n1. **Batch Processing**:\n   - Processes images in batches (default: 50) to optimize memory usage and handle large directories efficiently.\n   - Introduces a pause (`PAUSE_DURATION`) between batches to avoid system overload.\n\n2. **User Choice**:\n   - Allows users to choose between resizing large images, upscaling smaller ones, or both.\n   - Ensures flexibility based on specific requirements.\n\n3. **DPI Standardization**:\n   - Applies a consistent DPI of 300 for all processed images, suitable for professional printing.\n\n4. **Logging**:\n   - Automatically generates a detailed CSV log with the original size, final size, and status for each processed file.\n   - Log file is named based on the directory and timestamp for easy tracking.\n\n5. **Error Handling**:\n   - Skips unsupported or corrupt images and logs errors for review.\n\n6. **File Overwrite**:\n   - Saves processed files by overwriting the originals, ensuring the directory remains clean and organized.\n\n7. **Dynamic Thresholds**:\n   - Resizing is applied to images over 9MB, while upscaling is applied to smaller images to ensure quality.\n\n---\n\n### Sample CSV Output:\n| File               | Original Size (MB) | Final Size (MB) | Status                     |\n| ------------------ | ------------------ | --------------- | -------------------------- |\n| `image1.jpg`       | 12.4               | 8.9             | Processed ✅                |\n| `image2.png`       | 5.2                | 10.4            | Processed ✅                |\n| `corrupt_file.png` | N/A                | N/A             | Error - Unidentified Image |\n\n---\n\n### How It Runs:\n1. **User Input**:\n   - The script asks for the directory containing images.\n   - Users select a processing mode:\n     - `1`: Resize only large images (≥ 9MB).\n     - `2`: Resize large images and upscale smaller ones.\n     - `3`: Upscale small images only (< 9MB).\n\n2. **Batch Execution**:\n   - Images are processed in groups of 50 to prevent memory overload.\n   - The script resizes or upscales images based on the user's choice and the image size.\n\n3. **Log Generation**:\n   - After processing, the script writes a CSV log file in the source directory with detailed information about each image.\n\n---\n\n### Example Execution:\n```\n🔥 Welcome to the Ultimate Image Resizer & Upscaler 🔥\n📂 Enter the path to the source directory: /path/to/images\n🎯 Choose Processing Mode:\n1️⃣ Only resize images 9MB+ (Skip smaller ones)\n2️⃣ Resize 9MB+ & upscale anything smaller\n3️⃣ Only upscale images below 9MB (Ignore large ones)\n\n🔹 Enter 1, 2, or 3: 2\n\n📂 Processing Images in Directory: /path/to/images\n✨ Processing images ✨: 50%|███████████████████▌            | 25/50 [00:03<00:03]\n📜 Log saved as: /path/to/images/images_2025-01-29_1430.csv\n🎉 All images processed successfully! 🎊\n```\n\n---\n\n### Suggestions for Further Improvements:\n1. **Multi-Threading**:\n   -
